Text: Hyperbolic lattices are a revolutionary platform for tabletop simulations of holography and quan-, Font: CMR9, Size: 8.966400146484375
Text: tum physics in curved space and facilitate eﬃcient quantum error correcting codes. Their underlying, Font: CMR9, Size: 8.966400146484375
Text: geometry is non-Euclidean, and the absence of Bloch’s theorem precludes the straightforward ap-, Font: CMR9, Size: 8.966400146484375
Text: plication of the often indispensable energy band theory to study model Hamiltonians on hyperbolic, Font: CMR9, Size: 8.966400146484375
Text: lattices. Motivated by recent insights into hyperbolic band theory, we initiate a crystallography, Font: CMR9, Size: 8.966400146484375
Text: of hyperbolic lattices. We show that many hyperbolic lattices feature a hidden crystal structure, Font: CMR9, Size: 8.966400146484375
Text: characterized by unit cells, hyperbolic Bravais lattices, and associated symmetry groups. Using the, Font: CMR9, Size: 8.966400146484375
Text: mathematical framework of higher-genus Riemann surfaces and Fuchsian groups, we derive, for the, Font: CMR9, Size: 8.966400146484375
Text: ﬁrst time, a list of example hyperbolic, Font: CMR9, Size: 8.966400146484375
Text:  {, Font: CMSY9, Size: 8.966400146484375
Text: p, q, Font: CMMI9, Size: 8.966400146484375
Text: }, Font: CMSY9, Size: 8.966400146484375
Text:  lattices and their hyperbolic Bravais lattices, including, Font: CMR9, Size: 8.966400146484375
Text: ﬁve inﬁnite families and several graphs relevant for experiments in circuit quantum electrodynamics, Font: CMR9, Size: 8.966400146484375
Text: and topolectrical circuits. This dramatically simpliﬁes the computation of energy spectra of tight-, Font: CMR9, Size: 8.966400146484375
Text: binding Hamiltonians on hyperbolic lattices, from exact diagonalization on the graph to solving a, Font: CMR9, Size: 8.966400146484375
Text: ﬁnite set of equations in terms of irreducible representations. The signiﬁcance of this achievement, Font: CMR9, Size: 8.966400146484375
Text: needs to be compared to the all-important role played by conventional Euclidean crystallography, Font: CMR9, Size: 8.966400146484375
Text: in the study of solids. We exemplify the high potential of this approach by constructing and diago-, Font: CMR9, Size: 8.966400146484375
Text: nalizing ﬁnite-dimensional Bloch wave Hamiltonians. Our work lays the foundation for generalizing, Font: CMR9, Size: 8.966400146484375
Text: some of the most powerful concepts of solid state physics, crystal momentum and Brillouin zone,, Font: CMR9, Size: 8.966400146484375
Text: to the emerging ﬁeld of hyperbolic lattices and tabletop simulations of gravitational theories, and, Font: CMR9, Size: 8.966400146484375
Text: reveals the connections to concepts from topology and algebraic geometry., Font: CMR9, Size: 8.966400146484375
Text: Hyperbolic geometry plays a paramount role at the, Font: CMR10, Size: 9.962599754333496
Text: frontier of both theoretical and experimental physics., Font: CMR10, Size: 9.962599754333496
Text: It underlies holographic descriptions of strongly coupled, Font: CMR10, Size: 9.962599754333496
Text: systems and models for quantum chaos, quantum grav-, Font: CMR10, Size: 9.962599754333496
Text: ity, and quantum entanglement [1–4]. It is fundamental, Font: CMR10, Size: 9.962599754333496
Text: to modern computational many-body techniques [5–11], Font: CMR10, Size: 9.962599754333496
Text: and forms the basis for powerful quantum error correct-, Font: CMR10, Size: 9.962599754333496
Text: ing codes [12–16]., Font: CMR10, Size: 9.962599754333496
Text: Recent experimental realizations of, Font: CMR10, Size: 9.962599754333496

Text: responding non-Euclidean graphs are suited to be imple-, Font: CMR10, Size: 9.962599754333496
